<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="margin: 0"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 423pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: right"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><IMG SRC="tm1921842d1_ex99-1image001.jpg" ALT=""><BR></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><B>Kroger to Update Investors on How <I>Restock
Kroger</I> is<BR>
Right Framework to Reposition Business and </B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><B>Create Shareholder Value at Investor
Conference</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; background-color: white"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">Reconfirms 2019 Guidance on Identical Sales, Adjusted FIFO Operating
Profit, Adjusted EPS and Alternative Profit Streams</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; background-color: white"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">Sets Financial Targets for Continued Sales Improvement and Profitable
Growth in 2020</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; background-color: white"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">Announces Board of Directors Approved $1 Billion Share Repurchase
Authorization</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">CINCINNATI, November 5, 2019 &ndash;&nbsp;The
Kroger Co. (NYSE: KR) today will update investors on how the&nbsp;<I>Restock Kroger&nbsp;</I>framework is repositioning the company
to create value for shareholders, customers and associates at its Investor Conference at the New York Stock Exchange.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Kroger also announced the company&rsquo;s
Board of Directors has approved a $1 billion share repurchase program, replacing the existing authorization that has approximately
$546 million remaining.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&ldquo;<I>Restock Kroger</I>&nbsp;sets Kroger up for a stronger
future,&rdquo; said Rodney McMullen, Kroger&rsquo;s chairman and chief executive officer. &ldquo;Momentum is returning to our core
grocery business as a result of our customer obsession and renewed intensity around operational excellence, plus the asset-light,
margin rich alternative profit streams that enrich our core supermarket business. We look forward to sharing how these come together
at Kroger to create a path to consistently strong and attractive total shareholder return.&rdquo;&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Kroger reconfirmed its 2019 guidance on identical sales, adjusted
operating profit, adjusted earnings per diluted share, and alternative profit streams. The company also set financial targets for
2020.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&ldquo;As promised on our second quarter earnings call, Kroger
is using our Investor Conference to provide an update on our future expectations to create value for shareholders, including early
detailed guidance for 2020,&rdquo; said Gary Millerchip, Kroger&rsquo;s chief financial officer. &ldquo;Kroger&rsquo;s value creation
model is strong and durable. We are pleased to see identical store sales momentum is building and we expect this trend to continue
into 2020 and beyond. We are also delivering adjusted earnings per diluted share growth for our shareholders through the <I>Restock
Kroger</I> timeframe, supported by a disciplined approach to returning cash to investors.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1; Options: NewSection -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt; font-size: 10pt; text-align: right"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->1<!-- Field: /Sequence --></P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&ldquo;We are confident that<I>&nbsp;Restock Kroger</I>&nbsp;is
the right strategic framework for business growth in 2019 and 2020, and to position Kroger for long-term growth in the future,&rdquo;
said McMullen.&nbsp;&ldquo;We believe that the food industry is special and big enough for different models to coexist &ndash;
and Kroger&rsquo;s model will be one of them because, at Kroger, we are uniquely good at food. Kroger is food first and we believe
that no matter who you are, where you&rsquo;re from, how you shop or what you like to eat, everyone deserves to have fresh, affordable
and easy-to-enjoy food that tastes amazing. Kroger&rsquo;s ability to be America&rsquo;s food partner is our competitive advantage.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>Financial Strategy</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Kroger expects its financial model to deliver improving adjusted operating profit performance over time and continue to generate
strong free cash flow. The company expects this to translate into a consistently strong and attractive total shareholder return
through sustained net earnings growth and by returning cash to shareholders, via share repurchases and a growing dividend over
time. Maintaining a strong investment grade balance sheet is a key component of Kroger&rsquo;s financial model.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">The company defines free cash flow
as operating cash flow (before company-sponsored pension contributions), less capital expenditures, and excluding the cash tax
effect of the sale of strategic assets.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Kroger reduced net total debt by $1.3
billion over the last four quarters. Kroger's net total debt to adjusted EBITDA ratio is 2.46, compared to 2.59 a year ago. The
company's net total debt to adjusted EBITDA ratio target range is 2.30 to 2.50.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Earlier this year, Kroger increased
the dividend by 14 percent, from 56&cent; to 64&cent; per year, marking the 13<SUP>th</SUP> consecutive year of dividend increases.
The company&rsquo;s quarterly dividend has grown at a double-digit compound annual growth rate since it was reinstated in 2006.
The company continues to expect, subject to board approval, an increasing dividend over time.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>2019 Guidance</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="border-collapse: collapse; width: 85%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">
<TR STYLE="vertical-align: bottom">
    <TD STYLE="font-size: 10pt; text-align: center; padding-bottom: 1pt">&nbsp;</TD><TD STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; padding-bottom: 1pt">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid">IDS (%)</TD><TD STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; padding-bottom: 1pt">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid">EPS ($)</TD><TD STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; padding-bottom: 1pt">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid">Operating<BR>
 Profit ($B)</TD><TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; padding-bottom: 1pt">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><B>Tax Rate</B></P> <P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><B>Range**</B></P></TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="vertical-align: bottom; background-color: rgb(204,238,255)">
    <TD STYLE="width: 48%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; padding-bottom: 1pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Adjusted<SUP>*</SUP></FONT></TD><TD STYLE="width: 1%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; padding-bottom: 1pt">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD STYLE="width: 12%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; padding-bottom: 1pt">2.0% - 2.25%</TD><TD STYLE="width: 1%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; padding-bottom: 1pt">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD STYLE="width: 12%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; padding-bottom: 1pt">$2.15 - $2.25</TD><TD STYLE="width: 1%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; padding-bottom: 1pt">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD STYLE="width: 12%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; padding-bottom: 1pt">$2.9 - $3.0</TD><TD STYLE="width: 1%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; padding-bottom: 1pt">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD STYLE="width: 12%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; padding-bottom: 1pt">22.5% - 23.0%</TD></TR>
</TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">* Without adjusted items, if applicable; operating profit represents
FIFO Operating Profit</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">** These rates reflect typical tax adjustments and do not reflect
changes to the rate from the completion of income tax audit examinations, which cannot be predicted.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">The company expects capital investments,
excluding mergers, acquisitions and purchases of leased facilities to range between $3.0 and $3.2 billion in 2019.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 2 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt; font-size: 10pt; text-align: right"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->2<!-- Field: /Sequence --></P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>2020 Guidance</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">In 2020, Kroger expects:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; background-color: white"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">Identical sales growth, excluding fuel, to be greater than 2.25%.
</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; background-color: white"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">Alternative profit businesses to grow incremental operating profit
in the range of $125 to $150 million.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; background-color: white"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">Adjusted FIFO operating profit to range from $3.0 to $3.1 billion.
</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; background-color: white"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">Adjusted EPS to range from $2.30 to $2.40 per diluted share.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; background-color: white"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">Capital investments, excluding mergers, acquisitions, and purchases
of leased facilities, to range between $3.2 and $3.4 billion.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; background-color: white"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">Free cash flow to be in the range of $1.6 to $1.8 billion.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; background-color: white"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">To repurchase shares in the range of $500 million to $1 billion.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; background-color: white"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">A tax rate of approximately 23%.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><B>Beyond 2020</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">Kroger is targeting total shareholder
return of between 8% and 11% beyond 2020. This will be driven by 3% &ndash; 5% growth from improved earnings, and growth in the
company&rsquo;s free cash flow payout rate through a combination of share repurchases and dividends. This range excludes any potential
change in our price-to-earnings multiple, and the optionality for additional growth beyond 2020 created through strategic partnerships.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">At The Kroger Co. (NYSE: KR), we are
dedicated to our Purpose: to&nbsp;<B>Feed the Human Spirit<SUP>&reg;</SUP></B>. We are nearly half a million associates who serve
over 11 million customers daily through a seamless digital shopping experience and 2,759 retail food stores under a variety of&nbsp;<U>banner
names</U>, serving America through food inspiration and uplift, and creating #ZeroHungerZeroWaste communities by 2025. To learn
more about us, visit our&nbsp;<U>newsroom</U>&nbsp;and investor relations&nbsp;<U>site</U>.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">This press release includes forward-looking non-GAAP financial
measures, which&nbsp;management believes to be useful to investors and analysts.&nbsp;Kroger is unable to provide a full reconciliation
of the non-GAAP measures used in our&nbsp;2019 and 2020 guidance, including adjusted net earnings per diluted share&nbsp;to net
earnings per diluted share, adjusted FIFO operating profit to operating profit, and adjusted tax rate to tax rate,&nbsp;without
unreasonable effort&nbsp;because it is not possible to predict with a reasonable degree of certainty the information necessary
to calculate such measures on a GAAP basis. It is not possible to estimate with a reasonable degree of certainty&nbsp;certain of
our adjustment items because such information is&nbsp;dependent on future events&nbsp;that may be outside&nbsp;of our control.&nbsp;The
unavailable information could have a significant impact on&nbsp;2019 and 2020&nbsp;GAAP&nbsp;financial results.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"></P>

    <DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>

that compete with Kroger; pricing and promotional activities of existing and new competitors, including non-traditional competitors,
and the aggressiveness of that competition; Kroger's response to these actions; the state of the economy, including interest rates,
the inflationary and deflationary trends in certain commodities, changes in tariffs, and the unemployment rate; the effect that
fuel costs have on consumer spending; volatility of fuel margins; changes in government-funded benefit programs; manufacturing
commodity costs; diesel fuel costs related to Kroger's logistics operations; trends in consumer spending; the extent to which Kroger's
customers exercise caution in their purchasing in response to economic conditions; the uncertain pace of economic growth; changes
in inflation or deflation in product and operating costs; stock repurchases; Kroger's ability to retain pharmacy sales from third
party payors; consolidation in the healthcare industry, including pharmacy benefit managers; Kroger's ability to negotiate modifications
to multi-employer pension plans; natural disasters or adverse weather conditions; the potential costs and risks associated with
potential cyber-attacks or data security breaches; the success of Kroger's future growth plans; the ability to execute on <I>Restock
Kroger</I>; and the successful integration of merged companies and new partnerships. Our ability to achieve these goals may also
be affected by our ability to manage the factors identified above. Our ability to execute our financial strategy may be affected
by our ability to generate cash flow.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
